9-64 DECKLISTS
==============



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX SANTIAGO 2016](/en/events/coverage/gpsan16)
 on October 30, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/Neale.jpg)
By Neale Talbot











Following are the Top 63 decklists from GP Santiago, 2016. Alas, the 64th decklist has been lost to history.
